# crates/gcode/contract/gcode.contract.json

Module: [[code/modules/crates/gcode/contract|crates/gcode/contract]]

## Purpose

Defines the `gcode` CLI contract for Gobby: it records the tool name, contract version, and brief description, then lays out the shared `global_flags`, project `scope` resolution defaults and identity keys, and a large `commands` catalog. Each command entry combines its summary with accepted positionals, flags, daemon consumption behavior, and any JSON output keys, while the file ends by enumerating the CLI’s error codes.

[crates/gcode/contract/gcode.contract.json:5-49]
[crates/gcode/contract/gcode.contract.json:7]
